    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer14536556863686154793">I read this book on Wattpad a little while ago and I'm going to be honest, at first I thought I wasn't going to like it. Before I started reading it I thought it would be sickeningly cliché, and it was cliché, but it was a twist on a cliché if that makes sense O_o :) It was different and it really made me laugh (thanks to this book my family think I'm weirder than I am) and I was crying so much at some points. I loved Evelyn, she didn't really change for her man, she just got her act together. H</span>
  <span id="freeText14536556863686154793" style="display:none">I read this book on Wattpad a little while ago and I'm going to be honest, at first I thought I wasn't going to like it. Before I started reading it I thought it would be sickeningly cliché, and it was cliché, but it was a twist on a cliché if that makes sense O_o :) It was different and it really made me laugh (thanks to this book my family think I'm weirder than I am) and I was crying so much at some points. I loved Evelyn, she didn't really change for her man, she just got her act together. Hey, who doesn't love a badass? Awww, her teddy bear as well :') I highly recommend this book and I'd like to congratulate the author on getting it published :) peace out motherf*ckers ✌</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11780501109942000923">I peered over my friend's shoulder as she was on her phone in order to see what had captured her attention so tightly one day. On her screen was this book, off of Wattpad, and when I asked her what she was reading, she wouldn't answer me. Honestly, I don't think she even knew anyone was talking to her, she was so engrossed. She was reading this book, and then I ended up reading and falling in love with it as well. The title made is sound slightly cliché at first, but it was a good kind of cliché</span>
  <span id="freeText11780501109942000923" style="display:none">I peered over my friend's shoulder as she was on her phone in order to see what had captured her attention so tightly one day. On her screen was this book, off of Wattpad, and when I asked her what she was reading, she wouldn't answer me. Honestly, I don't think she even knew anyone was talking to her, she was so engrossed. She was reading this book, and then I ended up reading and falling in love with it as well. The title made is sound slightly cliché at first, but it was a good kind of cliché, if you know what I mean. I highly recommend you read this book, it makes me smile every time I think about it. </span>

I don't have that much time to waste.</span>

<div id="review_1985336550" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1985336550" />
    <a title="Cynthia Heyman" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13540102-cynthia-heyman"><img alt="Cynthia Heyman" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1985336550?book_show_action=true">May 06, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cynthia Heyman" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cynthia Heyman" href="/user/show/13540102-cynthia-heyman">Cynthia Heyman</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24143207-the-bad-girl-and-the-good-boy">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1985336550" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer236001814154566445"><strong>Another high school romance</strong><br/><br/> Yeah, I said it. But don't misunderstand me, I really enjoy this read! Ms. Luna's enthralling storytelling had me turning page after page. The title drew me in considering, it's always bad boy, good girl that gets center stage lately. The central characters and their counterpart s as well as really good plot and the ease with which Ms. Luna "speaks" to her audience. If you are looking for a good and a lovely story to get lost in, The bad Girl and Good Boy is a treat.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText12444798724465205390" style="display:none">This book is like nothing before. It's creative, a new chance to read from two very unlikely perspectives from two innovative characters who meet and fall in love. Meet Evelyn Jo, a spiteful yet sexy and rebellious young teenager who ends up in trouble and relocated to live with the Coin family. Where she ends up meeting young introverted yet intelligent young man who has the mussels of a jock but the heart of a child. Slowly these two teens come across many incidents where they are constantly being tested on their true feelings for each other. Can Zavier Coin pull enough courage to bring himself to speak to Evelyn Jo and tell her his true feelings? Can Evelyn leave all her troubles and finally fall in love with the shy but handsome Zavior Coin? Find out and read the exciting and thrilling book The Bad Girl And The Good Boy and find out!</span>

<div id="review_1823010341" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1823010341" />
    <a title="Rafaela Sousa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23217529-rafaela-sousa"><img alt="Rafaela Sousa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1490913404p2/23217529.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1823010341?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rafaela Sousa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rafaela Sousa" href="/user/show/23217529-rafaela-sousa">Rafaela Sousa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1823010341" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6583566111918130051">I'm giving this book two stars only because of the potencial that it had and the idea of portraying a true shy, introvert and self conscious boy who took baby steps and time to become a more confident and outgoing person, without changing into another complete different person or going from the shy guy to a sex god in three chapters. Growing up doesn't mean becoming another person all at once but a better version of yourself with all the experience that sometimes only time can give you, I'm glad</span>
  <span id="freeText6583566111918130051" style="display:none">I'm giving this book two stars only because of the potencial that it had and the idea of portraying a true shy, introvert and self conscious boy who took baby steps and time to become a more confident and outgoing person, without changing into another complete different person or going from the shy guy to a sex god in three chapters. Growing up doesn't mean becoming another person all at once but a better version of yourself with all the experience that sometimes only time can give you, I'm glad that it was what happened with Evelyn, and it's a powerfull message in the book. Overall I think this book could be a good one if rewriten with more care, with more plots and less repeated words, if it dived further into more complex definitions and explanations and were edited with more reflection. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6583566111918130051" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('sIbDjJA+yuu763ySSF0xoLqS16L5ZWvjPefeyHjWYfsL1CDeJZ2oSFJucLqAvGyqVYTnBJSeBq2oC6VHzzegdA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OFoT4KWaU076vXSggg8z/v3RAqrSOSxsrbJUSqAc1ICDCPCyEDkx7RM4eIhK7m70EscyDL/CQSI4Xi/FF/0VDw==')})
  }
